__quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n425:                                             const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n426:     {\n427:         for(int k =      // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale;\n            int Signed range is [-4, +3].\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecQ3 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Layout per quantization block (32 values = 8 threads * 4 fp16x2 lanes):\n    //  - each thread owns 8 values and writes:\n    //      * q2 payload : 8 * 2 bits -> uint16 (2 bytes)\n    //      * q1 payload : 8 * 1 bit  -> uint8  (1 byte)\n    //  - one scale is shared per 32 values and written by group leader.\n    //\n    // kRankTileStride is split as:\n    //   [0   .. 511] : q2 payload region (256 threads * 2 bytes)\n    //   [512 .. 767] : q1 payload region (256 threads * 1 byte)\n    //   [768 .. 895] : scale region (32 groups * 4 bytes)\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 896;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileQ1Offset        = 512;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 768;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // {-1/4.0h, -1/4.0h}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t.  // {1e-7, 1e-7}, f16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleEpsilon = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7;\n\n    // {-4, -4}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMin = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xC400C400 : 0xC080C080;\n\n    // {+3, +3}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMax = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x42004200 : 0x40404040;\n\n    // {+4, +4}, int16x2_t -- shifts signed [-4, +3] to unsigned [0, 7].\n    static constexpr int kRangeBias = 0x00040004;\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ3(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // 1) Per-group dynamic scale (shared across 32 values).\n            int wblockmax      = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // 2) Scale + clip to signed int3 range [-4, +3].\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // 3) Round to integer and bias to unsigned domain [0, 7].\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // 4) Split each 3-bit unsigned value into low-2-bit and high-1-bit\n            // halves, packed into one uint16 (low 2 bits per value) plus one\n            // uint8 (high 1 bit per value).\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            uint8_t q1w  = 0;\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    uint32_t v = static_cast<uint32_t>(tw[i]) & 0x7u;\n                    q2w |= static_cast<uint16_t>((v & 0x3u) << (i * 2));\n                    q1w |= static_cast<uint8_t>(((v >> 2) & 0x1u) << i);\n                }\n            }\n\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint8_t* q1w_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ1Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n            *q1w_ptr = q1w;\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint8_t* q1w_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ1Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            uint8_t q1w  = *q1w_ptr;\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack unsigned values [0, 7] then shift back to signed domain\n            // [-4, +3] by adding kRangeMin.\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                int16_t qv[8];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    uint32_t low2  = (q2w >> (2 * i)) & 0x3u;\n                    uint32_t high1 = (q1w >> i) & 0x1u;\n                    qv[i]          = static_cast<int16_t>(low2 | (high1 << 2));\n                }\n\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    int qpack = packed_from_int16_pair<T>(qv[2 * i], qv[2 * i + 1]);\n                    w[i]      = packed_add<T>(qpack, kRangeMin);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decode scale to reconstruct fp16/bf16 lanes.\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Int6 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Int6 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecQ6 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a int6x8_t (4B + 2B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 1664;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileQ2Offset        = 1024;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 1536;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // Constants configuration\n\n    // {-1/32.0h, -1/32.0h}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleFactor = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xA800A800 : 0xBD00BD00;\n\n    // {1e-7, 1e-7}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleEpsilon = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7;\n\n    // {-32, -32}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMin = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xD000D000 : 0xC200C200;\n\n    // {+31, +31}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMax = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x4FC04FC0 : 0x41F841F8;\n\n    // {+32, +32}, int16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeBias = 0x00200020;\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ6(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // Compute the absolute maximum of the atom in the thread group\n            // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale;\n            int encoding_scale;\n            decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // Convert from f16x2_t to uint16x2_t\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Pack 8 x q6 into int32_t + int16_t\n            uint32_t q4w;\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            q4w = (q[0] & 0x000F000F) | ((q[1] & 0x000F000F) << 4) | ((q[2] & 0x000F000F) << 8) |\n                  ((q[3] & 0x000F000F) << 12);\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    q2w |= (tw[i] >> 4) << (i * 2);\n                }\n            }\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q4w, q4w_ptr);\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint32_t q4w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q4w_ptr);\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack q6 into fp16x8_t\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                static uint constexpr kMask000F   = 0x000F000F;\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1024 = 0x64006400; // {1024.0, 1024.0}, fp16x2_t\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1056 = 0xE420E420; // {-1056.0, -1056.0}, fp16x2_t\n\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    int32_t q4 = q4w & kMask000F;\n                    int32_t q2 = (q2w & 0x3) | ((q2w & 0xC) << 14);\n                    q4w >>= 4;\n                    q2w >>= 4;\n                    if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                    {\n                        int32_t q6 = q4 | (q2 << 4) | kHalf2_1024;\n                        asm volatile(\"v_pk_add_f16 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i])\n                                     : \"v\"(q6), \"v\"(kHalf2_1056));\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        int32_t int16_2 = q4 | (q2 << 4);\n                        int16_t low     = static_cast<int16_t>(int16_2 & 0xFFFF);\n                        int16_t high    = static_cast<int16_t>((int16_2 >> 16) & 0xFFFF);\n\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Fp8 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Fp8 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecFP8 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static int constexpr kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a fp8x8_t (8B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 2176;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 2048;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0, \"kRankTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // FP8 Maximum value (on AMD Instinct MI300X - float8_e4m3fnuz)\n    static float constexpr kFP8Max = 240.0f;\n    static int constexpr kScaleFactor =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x1C441C44 : 0x3B883B88; // {1/240.0h, 1/240.0h}\n    static int constexpr kScaleEpsilon =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7; // {1e-7, 1e-7}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecFP8(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // abs(w)\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                T const* x = reinterpret_cast<T const*>(&atom);\n                T* y       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    y[i] = __habs(x[i]);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // max(w)\n            int wmax;\n            {\n                int a, b;\n                int* dw = reinterpret_cast<int*>(&w);\n                a       = packed_max<T>(dw[0], dw[1]);\n                b       = packed_max<T>(dw[2], dw[3]);\n                wmax    = packed_max<T>(a, b);\n\n                // Reduce the max among a group of 8 threads\n                // Note: This is basically 2 blocks of 32 values setup as the\n                // upper/lower halves of the fp16x2_t\n                for(int i = 1; i < 8; i <<= 1)\n                {\n                    int x = __shfl_down(wmax, i);\n                    wmax  = packed_max<T>(wmax, x);\n                }\n\n                // Share with the cohort\n                wmax = __shfl(wmax, group_leader);\n            }\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n            }\n\n            // Convert to packed FP8\n            fp32x8_t wf;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    half2 const* x = reinterpret_cast<half2 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y      = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __half22float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    nv_bfloat162 const* x = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y             = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __bfloat1622float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            int32x2_t qw;\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[0], wf[1], qw[0], 0);\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[2], wf[3], qw[0], 1);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[4], wf[5], qw[1], 0);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[6], wf[7], qw[1], 1);\n\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            int32x2_t qw = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qw_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack FP8\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 0])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf0[0]), \"v\"(wf0[1]));\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 1])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf1[0]), \"v\"(wf1[1]));\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    __hip_bfloat16* wbf = reinterpret_cast<__hip_bfloat16*>(&w);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 0]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 1]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[1]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 2]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 3]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[1]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Twoshot All Reduce\ntemplate <typename T, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half>\nstruct AllReduceTwoshot\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n\n    __device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                               T* __restrict__ output,\n                               uint32_t const N,                   // number of elements\n                               int const block,                    // block index\n                               int const rank,                     // rank index\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list, // communication buffers\n                               uint32_t const data_offset, // offset to start of the data buffer\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        // Topology\n        int thread           = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n        uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n        Codec codec(thread, rank);\n        int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n        uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n        for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        {\n            buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Read input into registers\n        int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                    half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1A: Write segment data into the communication buffer of the target\n        // rank responsible for this segment.\n        uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n        uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n\n        uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1B: Reduce the segment data from the communication buffers.\n        int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // note: we reuse tA as temp buffer here\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                {\n                    packed_assign_add<T>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Write the reduced segment to every other rank\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = The number of atoms per row that a thread touches is `atoms_per_thread_per_row = min(kAtoms, atoms_per_row / 256)` but wait...\n\nLet me just think of it as: for atom index `a` in the tile, the row is `a / atoms_per_row`.\nFor the i-th atom of thread t: `a_i = t + i * 256`.\nSince `t < 256`, and `atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / 8`:\n- `a_i / atoms_per_row = (t + i * 256) / atoms_per_row`\n\nFor the typical case where `atoms_per_row` is a multiple of 256 (hidden_dim is a multiple of 2048, which is true for 4096, 8192):\n`a_i / atoms_per_row = (t / atoms_per_row) + (i * 256 / atoms_per_row)`\n\nSince `t < 256 <= atoms_per_row` (for hidden_dim >= 2048), `t / atoms_per_row = 0`.\nSo `row_i = (i * 256) / atoms_per_row`.\n\nFor hidden_dim = 4096, atoms_per_row = 512:\n- i=0: row = 0\n- i=1: row = 256/512 = 0\n- i=2: row = 512/512 = 1\n- i=3: row = 768/512 = 1\n- i=4: row = 1024/512 = 2\n- i=5: row = 1280/512 = 2\n- i=6: row = 1536/512 = 3\n- i=7: row = 1792/512 = 3\n\nThis means row changes every 2 atoms. And importantly, the row assignment depends ONLY on `i` (the atom index within the thread), not on `t` (the thread index). This is great!\n\nSo for any thread, atoms 0,1 are in row 0; atoms 2,3 are in row 1; etc.\n\nActually wait, what about hidden_dim = 2048?\n- atoms_per_row = 256\n- rows_per_tile = 16384 / 2048 = 8\n- i=0: row = 0\n- i=1: row = 256/256 = 1\n- i=2: row = 512/256 = 2\n- ...\n- i=7: row = 1792/256 = 7\n\nEach atom is in a different row.\n\nWhat about hidden_dim = 8192?\n- atoms_per_row = 1024\n- rows_per_tile = 2\n- i=0..3: row = 0\n- i=4..7: row = 1\n\nSo the pattern varies, but since `hidden_dim` is a compile-time unknown but satisfies `kTileSize % (hidden_dim * sizeof(T)) == 0`, we know `atoms_per_row` divides `atoms_per_tile = 2048`, and `atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / 8`.\n\nAnd `kAtoms = 8` atoms per thread. Since `atoms_per_tile = 2048` and there are 256 threads, each thread handles 8 atoms. Since `atoms_per_row` divides 2048, and 256 divides 2048, the number of atoms per row per thread is `8 / rows_per_tile = 8 * hidden_dim * sizeof(T) / kTileSize`.\n\nFor hidden_dim = 4096: `8 * 4096 * 2 / 32768 = 2` atoms per row per thread.\nFor hidden_dim = 2048: `8 * 2048 * 2 / 32768 = 1` atom per row per thread.\nFor hidden_dim = 8192: `8 * 8192 * 2 / 32768 = 4` atoms per row per thread.\n\nSo each thread handles `atoms_per_row_per_thread = kAtoms / rows_per_tile` atoms from each row.\n\nNow for the RMSNorm reduction: I need the sum of squares per row. I can have each thread compute its partial sum of squares, then reduce within the row group.\n\nSince all threads in a block participate, and rows_per_tile could be up to 8 (for hidden_dim=2048), I need to reduce among threads that touch the same row.\n\nFor hidden_dim = 4096 (rows_per_tile = 4):\n- Row 0 is touched by all 256 threads (each touches 2 atoms in row 0)\n- Row 1 is touched by all 256 threads\n- etc.\n\nSo for each row, I need a reduction across all 256 threads. I can use shared memory: `__shared__ float row_ssq[8];` (max 8 rows). Then:\n1. Each thread computes its partial sum of squares for each row it touches\n2. All threads in the block reduce their partials into shared memory\n3. Each thread reads the final sum for the row of each atom it processes\n\nSince all 256 threads write to shared memory for each row, I need to be careful. I can do:\n```cpp\n__shared__ float row_ssq[8];\nfor(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++) {\n    float partial = 0.0f;\n    // compute partial for row r\n    for(int i = r * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i < (r+1) * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i++) {\n        // dequantize atom i, sum squares\n    }\n    // reduce partial across block\n    // using blockReduce or sequential shared memory\n}\n```\n\nWait, a simpler approach: since each row is touched by all threads, and the number of rows per tile is small (max 8), I can just have all threads participate in a block-level reduction for each row.\n\nIn fact, I can use `__syncthreads()` and have each thread add its partial to a shared memory accumulator:\n```cpp\n__shared__ float smem_ssq[8];\nif(thread == 0) {\n    for(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++) smem_ssq[r] = 0.0f;\n}\n__syncthreads();\n\nfor(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++) {\n    float partial = 0.0f;\n    for(int i = r * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i < (r+1) * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i++) {\n        // compute squares\n    }\n    atomicAdd(&smem_ssq[r], partial);\n}\n__syncthreads();\n```\n\nAtomicAdd on float in shared memory is fine on AMD GPUs. Since we have at most 8 rows and 256 threads, that's at most 8 * 256 = 2048 atomic operations, which is acceptable but maybe slow.\n\nA better approach: order the atoms so that threads in a warp/wavefront process the same row, then use warp shuffle. But looking at the atom layout, this isn't naturally the case — consecutive threads process consecutive atoms in the same row (for the first atom), but then the second atom jumps by 256 atoms.\n\nActually let me reconsider. For hidden_dim = 4096:\n- Atom 0 of thread t: `a = t`, row = 0\n- Atom 1 of thread t: `a = t + 256`, row = 0\n- Atom 2 of thread t: `a = t + 512`, row = 1\n...\n\nSo for row 0, the atoms are `t` and `t+256` for each thread t.\nFor row 1, the atoms are `t+512` and `t+768`.\n...\n\nConsecutive threads DO process consecutive atoms in the same row! Threads 0..255 process atoms 0..255 for row 0 (first atom), and atoms 256..511 for row 0 (second atom). So all 256 threads participate in row 0.\n\nA cleaner reduction: for each row, have threads compute partials, then do a tree reduction using shared memory.\n\n```cpp\n__shared__ float smem[256]; // one float per thread\nfor(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++) {\n    float partial = 0.0f;\n    for(int i = r * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i < (r+1) * atoms_per_row_per_thread; i++) {\n        // unpack atom i and accumulate squares\n    }\n    smem[thread] = partial;\n    __syncthreads();\n    \n    // block reduction\n    for(int stride = 128; stride > 0; stride /= 2) {\n        if(thread < stride) smem[thread] += smem[thread + stride];\n        __syncthreads();\n    }\n    float row_denom = rsqrtf(smem[0] / hidden_dim + eps);\n    __syncthreads();\n    // apply row_denom to atoms in row r\n}\n```\n\nThis is clean and efficient. 8 rows × ~8 reductions = very fast.\n\nNow, let me think about the actual data flow:\n\n1. After all-reduce phase 2, `tA[i]` (i=0..7) has the final all-reduced values in `CommT` format\n2. If `cast_bf2half=true`, `tA` is in half format, need to convert to `T` (bf16)\n3. For each atom, I also need to load the corresponding residual_inp and weight\n\nWait, the atom layout in `tA` is: atom `i` contains 8 `CommT` values (or half if cast). For the residual and weight, I should use the same style.\n\nActually, looking at the original code, it uses `BufferResource` for input and output. So I could load weight as `int32x4_t` and do packed multiplication.\n\nActually, let me simplify. Since the test tolerances are relatively loose (5e-3 for fp16, 4e-2 for bf16), I don't need the highest possible performance. But I do need to be faster than the unfused baseline by 2%. The main saving is avoiding the HBM round-trip, so even a straightforward implementation should win.\n\nLet me implement step by step:\n\n### Step 1: All-reduce communication\nThis is identical to `AllReduceTwoshot::run`, but using `CommT` for the codec. If `T == half` and `CommT == half`, same. If `T == bf16` and `CommT == bf16`, same.\n\nIf `T == bf16` and `CommT == half` and `cast_bf2half == true`:\n- Input loaded as bf16, converted to half in registers (`tA`)\n- All communication in half\n- After phase 2, `tA` has half data\n- Need to convert half->bf16 before adding bf16 residual\n\nSo in the fused kernel, after the all-reduce gather, I should conditionally convert `tA` from `CommT` to `T`:\n\n```cpp\nif constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n    // tA contains half, convert to bf16\n    for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n        const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n        nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n            float2 f = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n            bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n        }\n        tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nNow `tA` contains T (either half or bf16).\n\n### Loading residual and weight\n\nI'll use `BufferResource` for residual_inp, residual_out, output, and weight.\n\nWait, weight is a 1D buffer of `hidden_dim` elements. But the elements we need depend on the position within the row.\n\nFor atom `i` of thread `t`:\n- Global atom index: `block * atoms_per_tile + t + i * 256` (where `atoms_per_tile = kTileSize / sizeof(int32x4_t) = 2048`)\n- This is an element offset of `(block * atoms_per_tile + t + i * 256) * 8` elements\n- Within the row: `(t + i * 256) % atoms_per_row` atoms into the row\n- Weight offset in elements: `((t + i * 256) % atoms_per_row) * 8`\n\nSince `atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / 8`:\n- Weight offset: `((t + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)) * 8` bytes? No, elements.\n- In bytes: `((t + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)) * 8 * sizeof(T)`\n\nActually since `t < 256` and `hidden_dim / 8 >= 256` for `hidden_dim >= 2048`:\n- `(t + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)` \n- For `i = 0`: `t % (hidden_dim / 8) = t` (since t < 256 <= hidden_dim/8)\n- For `i = 1`: `(t + 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)`\n- etc.\n\nSo the weight offset isn't simply `t * 16` for all atoms. It changes per atom.\n\nFor simplicity, I'll just load weight atoms using `buffer_load_dwordx4` with the calculated offsets.\n\nActually, `weight` has `hidden_dim` elements. Since `hidden_dim * sizeof(T) <= kTileSize`, and we're processing `hidden_dim` elements per row, the weight buffer is much smaller than the data buffers. But we need to load weight elements multiple times (once per row in the tile).\n\nLet me set up a `BufferResource` for weight:\n```cpp\nBufferResource weight_buffer(const_cast<T*>(weight), hidden_dim * sizeof(T));\n```\n\nAnd for each atom `i`, the weight offset in bytes is:\n```cpp\nuint32_t weight_atom_idx = ((t + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / kElemsPerAtom));\nuint32_t weight_offset = weight_atom_idx * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n```\n\nWait, I need to be more careful. The `t` here is the thread index, which corresponds to the atom index within the tile. But `t` in `AllReduceTwoshot::run` is `threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront`.\n\nLet me use the same offset calculations as the original code.\n\nOriginal input load:\n```cpp\nuint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\nfor(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n    tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n    src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n}\n```\n\nSo the offset for atom `i` is: `block * kTileSize + thread * 16 + i * 256 * 16`\nIn elements: `block * elems_per_tile + thread * 8 + i * 256 * 8`\nIn atoms from start of tile: `thread + i * 256`\n\nFor weight, we need the offset within the weight buffer. Since weight is `hidden_dim` elements and each row uses the same weight:\n- Atom offset within the row: `(thread + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)`\n- Weight byte offset: `((thread + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)) * 16`\n\nFor `hidden_dim = 4096`, `hidden_dim / 8 = 512`:\n- Atom 0: `thread % 512 = thread` (since thread < 256)\n- Atom 1: `(thread + 256) % 512 = thread + 256`\n- Atom 2: `(thread + 512) % 512 = 0`? Wait, no, we want the weight for row 1. But weight is the same for all rows!\n- So yes, for atom 2 which is in row 1, the weight offset wraps around: `(thread + 512) % 512 = thread`\n\nSo the weight offset for atom `i` is simply `((thread + i * 256) % (hidden_dim / 8)) * 16`.\n\nAnd since `hidden_dim / 8` is a multiple of 256 (because `hidden_dim * sizeof(T)` divides `kTileSize = 32768`, so `hidden_dim` divides `16384`, and `hidden_dim / 8` divides `2048` which is a multiple of 256), the modulo can be computed as:\n`((thread + i * 256) % atoms_per_row)` where `atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / 8`.\n\nSince `atoms_per_row` is a power-of-2 multiple of 256? Actually it just needs to divide 2048. For hidden_dim = 4096, atoms_per_row = 512. For hidden_dim = 2048, atoms_per_row = 256. For hidden_dim = 8192, atoms_per_row = 1024.\n\nFor hidden_dim = 2048, atoms_per_row = 256, and thread < 256, so:\n- Atom 0: `thread % 256 = thread`\n- Atom 1: `(thread + 256) % 256 = thread`\n- Atom 2: `(thread + 512) % 256 = thread`\n- etc.\n\nAll atoms in all rows use the SAME weight elements! This makes sense because there are 8 rows per tile, but weight only has 2048 elements? Wait, hidden_dim = 2048, weight has 2048 elements. Each row has 2048 elements. So yes, all rows use the same weight.\n\nFor hidden_dim = 4096, atoms_per_row = 512:\n- Atom 0: `thread`\n- Atom 1: `thread + 256`\n- Atom 2: `thread` (since (thread+512)%512 = thread)\n- Atom 3: `thread + 256`\n- etc.\n\nGreat! So I can compute the weight offset per atom.\n\nBut actually, I realize there might be an easier way. Since `hidden_dim * sizeof(T)` divides `kTileSize`, and the tile contains an integer number of complete rows, and weight is the same for every row, I can just load weight once and reuse it. But with atoms wrapping around, I need to load each unique weight atom once.\n\nActually, the simplest approach: for each atom `i`, compute its position within the row, load the corresponding weight atom, do the multiply.\n\nLet me implement this step by step.\n\n### Implementation plan\n\n```cpp\n__device__ static void run(...) {\n    // 1. Setup (same as AllReduceTwoshot::run)\n    int thread = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n    uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n    Codec codec(thread, rank);\n    int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n    uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n    for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i) buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n\n    // 2. Read input into registers (tA)\n    BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n    uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n    \n    for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n        tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n        src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        if constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n            // convert bf16 input to half for communication\n            const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n            half2 half_buf[4];\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                float2 f = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n            }\n            tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 3. Phase-1A: Send\n    uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n    uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n    uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n    uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n    for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n        int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n        codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n    }\n\n    __syncthreads();\n    if(thread < kWorldSize) {\n        int r = thread;\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset + rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n    }\n\n    // 4. Phase-1B: Reduce\n    int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n    {\n        int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n            if(thread == 0) wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n            __syncthreads();\n            codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n            for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++) {\n                packed_assign_add<CommT>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 5. Phase-2: Write reduced segment to every other rank\n    for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n        int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n        codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n    }\n\n    __syncthreads();\n    if(thread < kWorldSize) {\n        int r = thread;\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags1_offset + rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n    }\n\n    // 6. Phase-2: Read gather segments\n    {\n        int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data1_offset);\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags1_offset);\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n            if(thread == 0) wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n            __syncthreads();\n            codec.recv(&recv_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 7. Convert tA from CommT to T if needed\n    if constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n            const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n            nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                float2 f = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n            }\n            tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // 8. At this point, tA contains all-reduced values in T format.\n    // Load residual_inp, add, write residual_out, compute sum of squares.\n    BufferResource res_buffer(const_cast<T*>(residual_inp), N * sizeof(T));\n    BufferResource res_out_buffer(residual_out, N * sizeof(T));\n    BufferResource weight_buffer(const_cast<T*>(weight), hidden_dim * sizeof(T));\n    BufferResource dst_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n\n    uint32_t res_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    uint32_t res_out_offset = res_offset;\n    uint32_t dst_offset = res_offset;\n\n    // We need to process atoms in the same order as the original.\n    // For RMSNorm, we need per-row sum of squares first, then apply.\n    \n    // Since we need to write residual_out before doing RMSNorm,\n    // and we need the row sums for RMSNorm, we'll:\n    // a) Load residual, add to tA, write residual_out, and accumulate squares in shared memory\n    // b) Reduce squares per row\n    // c) Load weight, apply normalization, write output\n\n    // But we can't easily re-read tA after writing. So:\n    // - First pass: load residual, add to tA, write residual_out, accumulate local sum of squares per row\n    // - Reduce per-row sums across block\n    // - Second pass: read weight, multiply tA by denom and weight, write output\n\n    __shared__ float smem_ssq[256]; // for block reduction, one per thread\n    const int rows_per_tile = (kTileSize / sizeof(T)) / hidden_dim;\n    const int atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / kElemsPerAtom;\n    \n    // Initialize partial sum of squares per row\n    // But we have 256 threads and small number of rows. We can store partials per thread per row in registers.\n    float row_ssq_partial[8] = {0.0f}; // max 8 rows\n    \n    for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n        // Load residual atom\n        int32x4_t res_atom = buffer_load_dwordx4(res_buffer.descriptor, res_offset, 0, 0);\n        \n        // Add element-wise: tA[i] = tA[i] + res_atom\n        // packed_assign_add<T> adds in-place to first arg, using second arg\n        // But we need to preserve tA for output. So compute sum in a temporary.\n        int32x4_t sum_atom;\n        if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value) {\n            // Use v_pk_add_f16 for each lane\n            const half2* a = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n            const half2* b = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&res_atom);\n            half2* s = reinterpret_cast<half2*>(&sum_atom);\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                asm volatile(\"v_pk_add_f16 %0, %1, %2\"\n                             : \"=v\"(*(int*)&s[j])\n                             : \"v\"(*(const int*)&a[j]), \"v\"(*(const int*)&b[j]));\n            }\n        } else {\n            const nv_bfloat162* a = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n            const nv_bfloat162* b = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&res_atom);\n            nv_bfloat162* s = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162*>(&sum_atom);\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                s[j] = __hadd2(a[j], b[j]);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        // Write residual_out\n        buffer_store_dwordx4(sum_atom, res_out_buffer.descriptor, res_out_offset, 0, 0);\n        \n        // Update tA to the sum for later output computation\n        tA[i] = sum_atom;\n        \n        // Accumulate sum of squares\n        T* sum_vals = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&sum_atom);\n        int atom_idx_within_tile = thread + i * kAtomStride;\n        int row_idx = atom_idx_within_tile / atoms_per_row;\n        float partial = 0.0f;\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; ++j) {\n            float v = qr_to_float<T>(sum_vals[j]);\n            partial += v * v;\n        }\n        row_ssq_partial[row_idx] += partial;\n        \n        res_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        res_out_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    }\n\n    // Block reduction for each row\n    __shared__ float smem_row_denom[8];\n    for(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++) {\n        smem_ssq[thread] = row_ssq_partial[r];\n        __syncthreads();\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int stride = 128; stride > 0; stride /= 2) {\n            if(thread < stride) {\n                smem_ssq[thread] += smem_ssq[thread + stride];\n            }\n            __syncthreads();\n        }\n        if(thread == 0) {\n            float mean_sq = smem_ssq[0] / float(hidden_dim);\n            smem_row_denom[r] = rsqrtf(mean_sq + eps);\n        }\n        __syncthreads();\n    }\n\n    // Second pass: apply weight and denom, write output\n    // Reset dst_offset\n    dst_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    \n    // Also need to reset weight offsets properly\n    for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n        int atom_idx_within_tile = thread + i * kAtomStride;\n        int row_idx = atom_idx_within_tile / atoms_per_row;\n        float denom = smem_row_denom[row_idx];\n        \n        // Load weight atom for this position within the row\n        int weight_atom_idx = atom_idx_within_tile % atoms_per_row;\n        uint32_t weight_offset = weight_atom_idx * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        int32x4_t weight_atom = buffer_load_dwordx4(weight_buffer.descriptor, weight_offset, 0, 0);\n        \n        // Multiply tA[i] by weight_atom and denom\n        int32x4_t out_atom;\n        if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value) {\n            const half2* x = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n            const half2* w = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&weight_atom);\n            half2* o = reinterpret_cast<half2*>(&out_atom);\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                // Convert to float, multiply, convert back\n                float2 xf = __half22float2(x[j]);\n                float2 wf = __half22float2(w[j]);\n                xf.x *= wf.x * denom;\n                xf.y *= wf.y * denom;\n                o[j] = __float22half2_rn(xf);\n            }\n        } else {\n            const nv_bfloat162* x = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n            const nv_bfloat162* w = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&weight_atom);\n            nv_bfloat162* o = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162*>(&out_atom);\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                float2 xf = __bfloat1622float2(x[j]);\n                float2 wf = __bfloat1622float2(w[j]);\n                xf.x *= wf.x * denom;\n                xf.y *= wf.y * denom;\n                o[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(xf);\n            }\n        }\n        \n        buffer_store_dwordx4(out_atom, dst_buffer.descriptor, dst_offset, 0, 0);\n        dst_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nHmm, there are a few issues with this approach:\n\n1. I'll keep the all-reduce part identical to `AllReduceTwoshot::run` (using CommT), then add the fused epilogue.\n\n```cpp\ntemplate <typename T, typename CommT, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half = false>\nstruct AllReduceTwoshotRMSNorm\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n    static_assert(sizeof(CommT) == 2);\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kElemsPerAtom = sizeof(int32x4_t) / sizeof(T);\n\n    __device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                               T const* __restrict__ residual_inp,\n                               T* __restrict__ residual_out,\n                               T* __restrict__ output,\n                               T const* __restrict__ weight,\n                               float eps,\n                               uint32_t const N,\n                               uint32_t const hidden_dim,\n                               int const block,\n                               int const rank,\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list,\n                               uint32_t const data_offset,\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        int thread = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n        uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n        Codec codec(thread, rank);\n        int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n        uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n        for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        {\n            buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Read input into registers\n        int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                    half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1A: Write segment data into the communication buffer of the target\n        // rank responsible for this segment.\n        uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n        uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n\n        uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1B: Reduce the segment data from the communication buffers.\n        int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // note: we reuse tA as temp buffer here\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                {\n                    packed_assign_add<CommT>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Write the reduced segment to every other rank\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags1_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Read the gather segments from the rank's communication buffer.\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data1_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags1_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // Gather all reduced and final rank segments into tA.\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Convert tA from CommT to T if needed\n        if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n        {\n            for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n            {\n                const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n                nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                    bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Fused epilogue: add residual, compute RMSNorm, write outputs\n        BufferResource res_buffer(const_cast<T*>(residual_inp), N * sizeof(T));\n        BufferResource res_out_buffer(residual_out, N * sizeof(T));\n        BufferResource weight_buffer(const_cast<T*>(weight), hidden_dim * sizeof(T));\n        BufferResource dst_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n\n        uint32_t res_offset     = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        uint32_t res_out_offset = res_offset;\n        uint32_t dst_offset     = res_offset;\n\n        const int rows_per_tile = (kTileSize / sizeof(T)) / hidden_dim;\n        const int atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / kElemsPerAtom;\n\n        // Partial sum of squares per row for this thread\n        float row_ssq_partial[8] = {0.0f};\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            // Load residual atom\n            int32x4_t res_atom = buffer_load_dwordx4(res_buffer.descriptor, res_offset, 0, 0);\n\n            // Add: sum = reduced + residual\n            int32x4_t sum_atom = tA[i];\n            packed_assign_add<T>(&sum_atom, &res_atom);\n\n            // Write residual_out\n            buffer_store_dwordx4(sum_atom, res_out_buffer.descriptor, res_out_offset, 0, 0);\n\n            // Update tA to the sum for the output pass\n            tA[i] = sum_atom;\n\n            // Accumulate sum of squares for the row this atom belongs to\n            int atom_idx_within_tile = thread + i * kAtomStride;\n            int row_idx              = atom_idx_within_tile / atoms_per_row;\n\n            T* sum_vals = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&sum_atom);\n#pragma unroll\n            for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; ++j)\n            {\n                float v = qr_to_float<T>(sum_vals[j]);\n                row_ssq_partial[row_idx] += v * v;\n            }\n\n            res_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            res_out_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        }\n\n        // Block-level reduction of sum of squares per row\n        __shared__ float smem_ssq[256];\n        __shared__ float smem_row_denom[8];\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < rows_per_tile; r++)\n        {\n            smem_ssq[thread] = row_ssq_partial[r];\n            __syncthreads();\n#pragma unroll\n            for(int stride = 128; stride > 0; stride >>= 1)\n            {\n                if(thread < stride)\n                {\n                    smem_ssq[thread] += smem_ssq[thread + stride];\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n            }\n            if(thread == 0)\n            {\n                float mean_sq = smem_ssq[0] / float(hidden_dim);\n                smem_row_denom[r] = rsqrtf(mean_sq + eps);\n            }\n            __syncthreads();\n        }\n\n        // Second pass: apply weight and denom, write output\n        dst_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            int atom_idx_within_tile = thread + i * kAtomStride;\n            int row_idx              = atom_idx_within_tile / atoms_per_row;\n            float denom              = smem_row_denom[row_idx];\n\n            int weight_atom_idx = atom_idx_within_tile % atoms_per_row;\n            uint32_t weight_offset = weight_atom_idx * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            int32x4_t weight_atom = buffer_load_dwordx4(weight_buffer.descriptor, weight_offset, 0, 0);\n\n            int32x4_t out_atom;\n            if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n            {\n                const half2* x = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n                const half2* w = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&weight_atom);\n                half2* o       = reinterpret_cast<half2*>(&out_atom);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 xf = __half22float2(x[j]);\n                    float2 wf = __half22float2(w[j]);\n                    xf.x *= wf.x * denom;\n                    xf.y *= wf.y * denom;\n                    o[j] = __float22half2_rn(xf);\n                }\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* x = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                const nv_bfloat162* w = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&weight_atom);\n                nv_bfloat162* o       = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162*>(&out_atom);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 xf = __bfloat1622float2(x[j]);\n                    float2 wf = __bfloat1622float2(w[j]);\n                    xf.x *= wf.x * denom;\n                    xf.y *= wf.y * denom;\n                    o[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(xf);\n                }\n            }\n\n            buffer_store_dwordx4(out_atom, dst_buffer.descriptor, dst_offset, 0, 0);\n            dst_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        }\n    }\n};\n```\n\nThis looks correct. Let me review once more:\n\n1. The all-reduce phases are identical to `AllReduceTwoshot::run`. \n2. After phase 2, `tA` has the gathered result in `CommT` format.\n3. If `cast_bf2half`, convert half -> bf16.\n4. Load residual, add in-place to `tA` copy, write to residual_out.\n5. Store sum back in `tA` for the output pass.\n6. Compute per-row sum of squares, reduce across block.\n7. Compute `denom = rsqrt(mean_sq + eps)`.\n8. Load weight, multiply `tA[i] * weight * denom`, write to output.\n\nOne thing: the buffer resource for `weight` is created with `hidden_dim * sizeof(T)`. The load offset is `weight_atom_idx * sizeof(int32x4_t)`. The buffer resource range is `hidden_dim * sizeof(T)`. The `buffer_load_dwordx4` instruction will load 16 bytes from `weight_offset`. If `weight_offset + 16 > hidden_dim * sizeof(T)`, it's out of bounds and returns 0. But since `weight_atom_idx = atom_idx_within_tile % atoms_per_row` and `atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / 8`, the maximum `weight_atom_idx` is `atoms_per_row - 1`, so `weight_offset = (atoms_per_row - 1) * 16 = hidden_dim * sizeof(T) / 8 * 8 - 16 = hidden_dim * sizeof(T) - 16`. So the last load is exactly the last 16 bytes, which is in bounds. Good.\n\nWait, `sizeof(int32x4_t) = 16`. Yes.\n\nAnother thing: `atom_idx_within_tile` is `thread + i * kAtomStride`. We need to convert each element to bf16 before the add/residual/norm operations.\n\nFor `cast_bf2half=false`, tA already contains T values and we can use them directly.\n\nNow let me carefully write the implementation.\n\n```cpp\n__device__ static void run(...) {\n    int thread = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n    uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n    Codec codec(thread, rank);\n    int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n    uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n    for(int i = 0; Write sum * denom * weight[col] to output[global_idx]\n\nI think the cleanest way is:\n\n```cpp\n// After all-reduce phase, values are in tA.\n\n// Step 1: Compute local per-row sum of squares and write residual_out\n// We'll reuse tA to store the (reduced + residual) values in T format.\n\n// But first, convert tA to T if cast_bf2half\nif constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n    for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n        half* h = reinterpret_cast<half*>(&tA[i]);\n        T* t = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[i]);\n        for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; j++) {\n            t[j] = qr_from_float<T>(__half2float(h[j]));\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Now tA contains T values.\n\nuint32_t elems_per_tile = kTileSize / sizeof(T);\nuint32_t tile_base = block * elems_per_tile;\nuint32_t rows_per_tile = elems_per_tile / hidden_dim;\n\n// Local per-row sum of squares\nfloat local_sq = 0.0f; // We'll track for each row separately\n\n// But we have multiple rows. Use shared memory for row sums.\n__shared__ float smm_sq[512]; // max possible rows_per_tile\n\nfor(int r = thread; r < rows_per_tile; r += kBlockSize) {\n    smm_sq[r] = 0.0f;\n}\n__syncthreads();\n\n// Process each atom\nfor(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n    uint32_t base_elem = thread * kElemsPerAtom + i * kAtomStride * kElemsPerAtom;\n    uint32_t global_idx = tile_base + base_elem;\n    uint32_t row_in_tile = base_elem / hidden_dim;\n    uint32_t col = base_elem % hidden_dim;\n    \n    T* atom_t = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[i]);\n    \n    for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; j++) {\n        if(global_idx + j < N) {\n            float reduced_val = qr_to_float<T>(atom_t[j]);\n            float residual_val = qr_to_float<T>(residual_inp[global_idx + j]);\n            float sum = reduced_val + residual_val;\n            \n            // Write residual_out\n            residual_out[global_idx + j] = qr_from_float<T>(sum);\n            \n            // Accumulate sum^2\n            // atomic add to smm_sq[row_in_tile]\n            // But j might cross a row boundary? No, kElemsPerAtom=8 and hidden_dim is large.\n            // Wait, col + j might exceed hidden_dim? No, because base_elem % hidden_dim + j < hidden_dim?\n            // Actually base_elem = thread * 8 + i * 2048. col = base_elem % hidden_dim.\n            // If col is near hidden_dim, col + 7 might exceed hidden_dim.\n            // BUT: since hidden_dim is a multiple of kElemsPerAtom (probably, as power of 2, and kElemsPerAtom=8),\n            // and the access pattern is aligned... Let me check.\n            // thread * 8 is always a multiple of 8. i * 2048 is a multiple of 8. So base_elem is a multiple of 8.\n            // If hidden_dim is a multiple of 8, then col is a multiple of 8, and col + 7 < hidden_dim.\n            // But is hidden_dim always a multiple of 8? The problem says power of 2 like 4096/8192, so yes.\n            // However, to be safe, we can handle the boundary case.\n            \n            atomicAdd(&smm_sq[row_in_tile], sum * sum);\n            \n            // Alternatively, use a local accumulator and do one atomicAdd per atom\n            \n            // Actually, let me batch: for an entire atom, all elements are in the same row\n            // since hidden_dim >= kElemsPerAtom and col + kElemsPerAtom - 1 < hidden_dim.\n            \n            atom_t[j] = qr_from_float<T>(sum); // save back to tA for output pass\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n__syncthreads();\n\n// Compute denom per row\nfor(int r = thread; r < rows_per_tile; r += kBlockSize) {\n    float mean_sq = smm_sq[r] / float(hidden_dim);\n    smm_sq[r] = rsqrtf(mean_sq + eps); // reuse smm_sq as denom\n}\n__syncthreads();\n\n// Step 2: Write output\nfor(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n    uint32_t base_elem = thread * kElemsPerAtom + i * kAtomStride * kElemsPerAtom;\n    uint32_t global_idx = tile_base + base_elem;\n    uint32_t row_in_tile = base_elem / hidden_dim;\n    uint32_t col = base_elem % hidden_dim;\n    \n    T* atom_t = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[i]);\n    float denom = smm_sq[row_in_tile];\n    \n    for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; j++) {\n        if(global_idx + j < N) {\n            float sum = qr_to_float<T>(atom_t[j]);\n            float w = qr_to_float<T>(weight[col + j]);\n            float out_val = sum * denom * w;\n            output[global_idx + j] = qr_from_float<T>(out_val);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, using `atomicAdd` 8 times per thread on shared memory could be slow. Let me optimize.\n\nBetter: use local accumulator per atom, then atomicAdd once per atom.\n\n```cpp\nfor(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n    uint32_t base_elem = thread * kElemsPerAtom + i * kAtomStride * kElemsPerAtom;\n    uint32_t global_idx = tile_base + base_elem;\n    uint32_t row_in_tile = base_elem / hidden_dim;\n    uint32_t col = base_elem % hidden_dim;\n    \n    T* atom_t = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[i]);\n    float atom_sq = 0.0f;\n    \n    for(int j = 0; j < kElemsPerAtom; j++) {\n        if(global_idx + j < N) {\n            float reduced_val = qr_to_float<T>(atom_t[j]);\n            float residual_val = qr_to_float<T>(residual_inp[global_idx + j]);\n            float sum = reduced_val + residual_val;\n            residual_out[global_idx + j] = qr_from_float<T>(sum);\n            atom_sq += sum * sum;\n            atom_t[j] = qr_from_float<T>(sum);\n        }\n    }\n    \n    atomicAdd(&smm_sq[row_in_tile], atom_sq);\n}\n```\n\nActually, even better: we can avoid atomicAdd entirely if we structure the reduction properly.\n\nSince all threads in the block process all rows, each row gets exactly `kBlockSize * (kAtoms / rows_per_tile) * kElemsPerAtom` elements. Each thread reads/writes its own tA[i].
